Disadvantages: Chinese restaurants tend to rip off customers, with all sorts of inexplicable charges, and guests are not informed before the meal. In addition, the menu is just a printed white paper with no prices. We ate nearly 800 for 3 meat dishes and 2 vegetarian dishes. We were charged service fees, taxes, and tea table fees. The most annoying thing is that even children were charged tea table fees. Please avoid this trap.
       There is a charge for the minibar. The hotel price is nearly 2k during the Spring Festival, which is a bit pricey. Breakfast can only be said to be quite satisfactory, a little simple.
       There is no online car-hailing service in Fenghuang Ancient City and the high-speed rail shuttle bus only goes to the ancient city. The hotel is still about 2 kilometers away from the ancient city. It is impossible to get a taxi during the Spring Festival holiday. This section is very troublesome. I took my children and carried the luggage for a long time before arriving. Yes, very tired. It might be better to take a taxi during the off-season.

The hotel has a rich breakfast, and there are Chinese and Western restaurants for dinner. We tried them both during our two-day stay. Chinese restaurants charge more items. In contrast, the buffets in Western restaurants are reasonably priced and more cost-effective. They include steaks and mutton chops, various fish sashimi, green prawns and crabs and other seafood, as well as various meat and vegetable Chinese dishes. However, during the stay, the air conditioner in the room only had fresh air mode and could not adjust the cooling. It still felt a bit stuffy. As a Wyndham hotel chain, this needs to be improved. In addition, the hotel does not seem to have an executive lounge, so it seems difficult to enjoy the executive lounge benefits of some room types.
